      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (minimal Anaconda) for flexibility and multiple Python versions support
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Create conda environment named kilosort with python 3.11 (latest supported)
  RUN conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.11 && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Activate environment and install dependencies
  # Copy setup.py to working dir for pip install
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  # Install pip packages inside the conda environment
  # Install core dependencies including cpu-only torch
  # Install GUI extras and docs/testing extras optionally
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      # Upgrade pip first \
      pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      # Install core dependencies explicitly to ensure CPU-only PyTorch \
      pip install numpy>=1.20.0 scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu torch cpuonly && \
      # Install GUI extras \
      pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      # Install docs extras \
      pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      # Install testing tools \
      pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      # Install Kilosort package with GUI extras \
      pip install .[gui]"
  # Copy docs requirements.txt for optional docs dependencies install
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  # Install docs requirements from requirements.txt (nbsphinx, myst_parser, sphinx_rtd_theme)
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install -r docs/requirements.txt"
  # Copy tox.ini and pytest.ini for testing configuration
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  # Copy docs Makefile and make.bat for building docs
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  # Copy docs conf.py for documentation build configuration
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  # Copy .readthedocs.yml file for Read the Docs configuration
  COPY .readthedocs.yml .readthedocs.yml
  # Ensure all other repository files are copied (except for large optional folders if .dockerignore used)
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables to avoid GPU usage and CUDA dependencies
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  # Default to bash shell with conda environment activated
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && exec /bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_071208_tensorblock_gpt-4.1-mini/Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Update conda to latest version
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y"
  # Debug info for conda before environment creation
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda info && conda config --show"
  # Create conda environment named kilosort with python 3.11
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.11 && conda clean -afy"
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu torch cpuonly && \
      pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      pip install .[gui]"
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install -r docs/requirements.txt"
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY .readthedocs.yml .readthedocs.yml
  COPY . .
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && exec /bin/bash"]

      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \

      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN /bin/bash -c "$CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.11 && conda clean -afy"
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu torch cpuonly && \
      pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      pip install .[gui]"
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install -r docs/requirements.txt"
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY .readthedocs.yml .readthedocs.yml
  COPY . .

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.11 && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu torch cpuonly && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install .[gui]
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY .readthedocs.yml .readthedocs.yml
  COPY . .
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && exec /bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --show && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda info && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort -c conda-forge python=3.11 && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu torch cpuonly && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install .[gui]
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY .readthedocs.yml .readthedocs.yml
  COPY . .
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && cd /Kilosort4 && exec /bin/bash"]

      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.11 && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY .readthedocs.yml .readthedocs.yml
  COPY . .
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install .[gui] && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && cd /Kilosort4 && exec /bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "kilosort", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu
  RUN pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu
  RUN pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib
  RUN pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme
  RUN pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py
  RUN pip install .[gui]
  RUN pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  CMD ["conda", "run", "-n", "kilosort", "/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda init bash
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "kilosort", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu
  RUN pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu
  RUN pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib
  RUN pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme
  RUN pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py
  RUN pip install .[gui]
  RUN pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  CMD ["conda", "run", "-n", "kilosort", "/bin/bash"]

Python 3.9, 3.10, and 3.11 compatibility remain supported for Read the Docs and testing. Paths reflect working directory `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_071208_tensorblock_gpt-4.1-mini/Kilosort4`.
  ---
  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:  
     - Anaconda Python distribution (https://www.anaconda.com/products/distribution), supporting Python 3.9, 3.10, or 3.11 (for Read the Docs build compatibility)  
     - Git client (https://git-scm.com/downloads) for cloning repository  
     - Pandoc (https://pandoc.org/) - required for markdown conversion in documentation builds  
     - Optional: Jupyter Notebook or JupyterLab (via conda or pip) for notebook support  
     - Optional: Phy GUI for manual spike sorting curation (https://github.com/cortex-lab/phy)  
     - Python package dependencies as defined in `setup.py`:  
       - Core: numpy (≥1.20.0), scipy, scikit-learn, tqdm, torch (≥1.6), numba, faiss-cpu  
         - **Note:** Install CPU-only PyTorch version since no GPU is available  
       - GUI extras: pyqtgraph (≥0.13.0), qtpy, pyqt6 and pyqt6.sip (or pyqt5/pyqt5.sip, or PySide2/PySide6 depending on system), matplotlib  
       - Documentation extras: sphinx (≥3.0), sphinxcontrib-apidoc, nbsphinx, myst_parser, sphinx_rtd_theme, pandoc  
       - Testing tools: pytest (including pytest-cov, pytest-xvfb), py (for test execution and coverage)  
     - Note on PyQt and Qt bindings: Installer detects existing Qt backends and adjusts GUI dependencies accordingly  
     - tox configured for automated testing across Python versions (3.9, 3.10, 3.11) on Linux, macOS, Windows  
     - pytest.ini filters out DeprecationWarnings during test runs  
     - Sphinx documentation build tools with Makefile (Unix) and make.bat (Windows) scripts  
     - Network access required during docs build to download external README.md (via `docs/conf.py`)  
     - Python 3.11 support included for Read the Docs compatibility  
  ---
  2. FILES TO CREATE (relative to `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_071208_tensorblock_gpt-4.1-mini/Kilosort4`):  
     - Optional conda environment activation scripts: `activate_kilosort.sh` or `.bat`  
     - `params.py` user-generated Phy config in results folder  
     - Optional: Clone `Kilosort/` repo folder if developing

     - Optional: Custom probe `.mat` files  
     - Optional: `README.md` (auto-downloaded by `docs/conf.py` during doc build)

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install .[gui] && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/kilosort/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  # Initialize conda for bash and create environment with verbose output
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10 --verbose
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  RUN source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu && \
      pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu && \
      pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      pip install .[gui] && \
      pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/kilosort/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN eval "$($CONDA_DIR/bin/conda shell.bash hook)" && \
      conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10 --verbose
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  RUN eval "$($CONDA_DIR/bin/conda shell.bash hook)" && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu && \
      pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu && \
      pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      pip install .[gui] && \
      pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/kilosort/bin:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10 --verbose && \
      conda activate kilosort && \
      pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu && \
      pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu && \
      pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy pyqt6 pyqt6.sip matplotlib && \
      pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme && \
      pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py && \
      pip install .[gui] && \
      pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/kilosort/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=kilosort
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  WORKDIR /Kilosort4

      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10 --verbose && \
      conda run -n kilosort pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      conda run -n kilosort pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu && \

      conda run -n kilosort pip install .[gui] && \
      conda run -n kilosort pip install -r docs/requirements.txt
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""

  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=kilosort
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libxrender1 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      pandoc \
      make \
      xvfb \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile
  COPY docs/make.bat docs/make.bat
  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py
  COPY . .
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda create -y -n kilosort python=3.10 --verbose
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install 'numpy>=1.20.0' scipy scikit-learn tqdm numba faiss-cpu"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && conda install -y -c pytorch cpuonly pytorch"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && conda install -y pyqt matplotlib"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install pyqtgraph>=0.13.0 qtpy"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install sphinx>=3.0 sphinxcontrib-apidoc nbsphinx myst_parser sphinx_rtd_theme"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install pytest pytest-cov pytest-xvfb py"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install .[gui]"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate kilosort && pip install -r docs/requirements.txt"
  ENV CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=""
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/kilosort/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=kilosort
  WORKDIR /Kilosort4
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive

      wget \
      curl \
      git \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \

      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /bin/bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y || true
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda config --set channel_priority strict
  COPY setup.py setup.py
  COPY docs/requirements.txt docs/requirements.txt
  COPY tox.ini tox.ini
  COPY pytest.ini pytest.ini
  COPY docs/Makefile docs/Makefile

  COPY docs/conf.py docs/conf.py

      source $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
